Conclusion: 这项工作为使用贝叶斯统计高效校准手征有效场论核子相互作用铺平了道路，该方法可应用于其他核散射过程和有限量子系统。

Abstract: Nucleon-deuteron ($Nd$) scattering can be used to constrain three-nucleon forces in chiral effective field theory ($χ$EFT). However, high-fidelity calculations, such as the Hyperspherical Harmonic (HH) method, are computationally expensive, making it difficult or even prohibitive to explore the vast parameter space of $χ$EFT\xspace. To address this challenge, specifically for proton-deuteron ($pd$) scattering below the deuteron breakup threshold, we developed model-driven emulators based on the Reduced Basis Method (RBM) and active learning techniques, as presented in \href{https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01844}{arXiv:2511.01844}. The method exploits the similarities between solutions at different parameter points to significantly reduce computational costs. In this companion paper, we provide a comprehensive description of our HH-based high-fidelity calculations and implementation of both variational-method-based and Galerkin-projection-based scattering emulators. We demonstrate the effectiveness of active learning in the form of greedy algorithms for selecting optimal training points in the parameter space, and the high accuracy and speed of the emulators, for two different nucleon forces and two scattering channels (${1/2}^+$ and ${1/2}^-$). For example, in a two-dimensional parameter space, the relative emulation errors can be reduced to $10^{-7}$ with fewer than 10 training points. Our work paves the way for the efficient calibration of $χ$EFT\xspace nucleon interactions using Bayesian statistics, and the methodology can be applied to other nuclear scattering processes (including neutron-deuteron scattering), as well as other finite quantum systems.

</details>


### [159] [Friction terms in multi-fluid description of heavy-ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10487)
*Clemens Werthmann,Iurii Karpenko,Pasi Huovinen*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文比较了重离子碰撞多流体描述中不同的摩擦项推导方法，提出了一种新的"电荷转移"摩擦项，并在MUFFIN模型中实现，首次展示了粘性多流体动力学结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多流体描述中，摩擦项可以从动力学理论推导但不唯一，需要比较不同方法并找到更符合动量空间分离假设的摩擦项。

Method: 比较不同摩擦项推导方法，引入新的电荷转移摩擦项，在MUFFIN模型中实现，并采用粘性多流体动力学方法。

Result: 电荷转移摩擦项更符合三流体在动量空间清晰分离的假设，能更好地比较实验数据和基础状态方程，并为单个流体中的耗散熵生成留出空间。

Conclusion: 新提出的电荷转移摩擦项在多流体描述中具有更好的理论一致性和实用性，为粘性多流体动力学研究提供了新途径。

Abstract: In multi-fluid description of heavy-ion collisions, the primary scatterings and particle production are described in terms of interaction between fluids, so called friction. These friction terms can be derived from kinetic theory, but they are not unique. We compare different approaches to derive the friction terms, introduce a new ``charge transfer" friction, which allows to move charge to the midrapidity fireball, and implement them in the MUFFIN model. The charge transfer friction is more consistent with the assumption of three fluids clearly separated in momentum space, and allows better comparisons of the experimental data and underlying equation of state. It also leaves room for entropy generation due to dissipation in individual fluids, and we present the first results obtained using viscous multi-fluid dynamics.

</details>


### [160] [Non-Resonant Alpha-Induced Neutron-Emission: A Multi- Method Comparison Of Nuclear Reaction Rates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10536)
*Bhavay Luthra,N. J. Upadhyay*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该研究采用分析、理论和计算方法精确计算α诱导中子发射反应速率，通过蒙特卡洛方法验证并开发了计算代码，比较了不同方法对温度的依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确计算α诱导中子发射反应速率对于理解不同恒星环境中的核合成过程至关重要。

Method: 采用文献中的分析表达式，实施蒙特卡洛方法，并开发自己的计算代码来验证方法功能。

Result: 通过绘制反应速率对温度的依赖性，展示了各种方法计算结果的全面比较。

Conclusion: 研究为α诱导中子发射反应速率的精确计算提供了多种方法的验证和比较，有助于更好地理解恒星核合成过程。

Abstract: The precise calculation of alpha-induced neutron-emission ($α$,n) reaction rates is fundamental to understanding nucleosynthesis in diverse stellar environments. This study investigates the nuclear reaction rates for various non-resonant alpha-induced neutron-emission reactions by employing analytical, theoretical, and computational methods. We have adopted analytical expressions from existing literature, and for the computational approach, we have implemented the Monte Carlo method. To better understand the functionality and validate the established open-source Monte Carlo scripts, we also developed our own computational code and used it to test various aspects of the method. A comprehensive comparison of the reaction rates from each method is presented by plotting their dependency on temperature.

</details>
